	OutputLine(NULL, "「…………何が……どうなって……………。」",
		   NULL, "\"........ cosa... sta succedendo...?\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacter(1, 6, "sprite/si1a_warai_a1_", "2", -160, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 200, TRUE );

//「じゃ、行こ＠　圭ちゃん＠　もう暗くなってきたから、お家まで送ってあげるね＠お姉、悪いけど興宮の家に電話して車を回すように言ってもらえる＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s19/06/500600348", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「じゃ、行こ！",
		   NULL, "\"Allora ce ne andiamo!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s19/06/500600349", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　圭ちゃん！",
		   NULL, " Kei-chan!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s19/06/500600350", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　もう暗くなってきたから、お家まで送ってあげるね。",
		   NULL, " È già buio, quindi ti accompagno a casa.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s19/06/500600351", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "お姉、悪いけど興宮の家に電話して車を回すように言ってもらえる？",
		   NULL, " Sorellona, scusa ma non è che potresti telefonare alla casa di Okinomiya e chiedere di mandarci un'auto?", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　自転車も積めるように、ワゴンか何かで来てほしいって伝えてね。＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s19/06/500600352", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　自転車も積めるように、ワゴンか何かで来てほしいって伝えてね。」",
		   NULL, "Meglio un furgoncino, così da poterci caricare anche la bici, grazie.\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　嬉々満面の詩音と対照的な...半涙で抜け殻のようになった魅音￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　嬉々満面の詩音と対照的な…半涙で抜け殻のようになった魅音。",
		   NULL, "Al contrario di Shion, che sprizza gioia da tutti i pori... Mion è come un guscio vuoto che potrebbe scoppiare a piangere da un momento all'altro.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacter(3, 3, "sprite/me2_yowaki_a1_", "1", 160, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 20, 200, TRUE );

//「......ぅぅ............圭ちゃ～...ん...。＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>魅音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Mion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 3, "ps3/s19/03/500300223", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「……ぅぅ…………圭ちゃ〜…ん…。」",
		   NULL, "\"...... uuh...... Kei-cha~... n...\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　その後、別れるまで魅音のぼやきは絶えることはなかった...￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　その後、別れるまで魅音のぼやきは絶えることはなかった…。",
		   NULL, "E così, ci sorbiamo le lamentele di Mion finché non ci vengono a prendere...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//■５日目幕間

	Wait( 2000 );

	Wait( 1000 );

	DrawScene("black", 3000 );

	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	DrawSceneWithMask("tips/wata005", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );
